 // Lower 4 bits\n  uint64_t overflow_value = position >> 4;  // Upper bits\n\n  {\n    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n\n    // Update dense bucket if new value is larger\n    if (dense_value > dense_bucket_[bucket_idx].to_ullong()) {\n      dense_bucket_[bucket_idx] = std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(dense_value);\n\n      // Update overflow bucket if this is a new maximum\n      if (overflow_bucket_.find(bucket_idx) == overflow_bucket_.end() ||\n          overflow_value > overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx].to_ullong()) {\n        overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(overflow_value);\n      }\n    } else if (dense_value == dense_bucket_[bucket_idx].to_ullong() &&\n               overflow_value > 0) {\n      // If dense values are equal, update overflow if new overflow is larger\n      if (overflow_bucket_.find(bucket_idx) == overflow_bucket_.end() ||\n          overflow_value > overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx].to_ullong()) {\n        overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(overflow_value);\n      }\n    }\n  }\n}\n\ntemplate <typename T>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<T>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  if (n_leading_bits_ <= 0) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n\n  uint64_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n_leading_bits_;\n\n  // Compute the harmonic mean using dense buckets and overflow buckets\n  double sum = 0.0;\n  for (uint64_t i = 0; i < num_buckets; ++i) {\n    uint64_t dense_val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n    uint64_t overflow_val = 0;\n\n    if (overflow_bucket_.find(i) != overflow_bucket_.end()) {\n      overflow_val = overflow_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n    }\n\n    // Reconstruct the position\n    uint64_t position = dense_val | (overflow_val << 4);\n\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(position));\n  }\n\n  // Apply the HyperLogLog formula\n  double raw_estimate = CONSTANT * num_buckets * num_buckets / sum;\n\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(raw_estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<std::string>;\n}  // namespace bustub\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":24,"oldLines":9,"newStart":24,"newLines":6,"lines":[" ","   // Compute the remaining bits (upper bits after removing bucket index bits)","   hash_t remaining_hash = hash >> (n_leading_bits_ > 0 ? n_leading_bits_ : 0);","-  if (remaining_hash == 0) {","-    remaining_hash = 1;  // All zeros = infinite leading zeros\n  } else {\n    // Count leading zeros from MSB\n    for (uint64_t i = 0; i < 64; ++i) {\n      if ((remaining_hash >> (63 - i)) & 1) {\n        position = i + 1;\n        break;\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Split position into dense (lower 4 bits) and overflow (upper bits) parts\n  uint64_t dense_value = position & 0xF;  // Lower 4 bits\n  uint64_t overflow_value = position >> 4;  // Upper bits\n\n  {\n    std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n\n    // Update dense bucket if new value is larger\n    if (dense_value > dense_bucket_[bucket_idx].to_ullong()) {\n      dense_bucket_[bucket_idx] = std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(dense_value);\n\n      // Update overflow bucket if this is a new maximum\n      if (overflow_bucket_.find(bucket_idx) == overflow_bucket_.end() ||\n          overflow_value > overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx].to_ullong()) {\n        overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(overflow_value);\n      }\n    } else if (dense_value == dense_bucket_[bucket_idx].to_ullong() &&\n               overflow_value > 0) {\n      // If dense values are equal, update overflow if new overflow is larger\n      if (overflow_bucket_.find(bucket_idx) == overflow_bucket_.end() ||\n          overflow_value > overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx].to_ullong()) {\n        overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(overflow_value);\n      }\n    }\n  }\n}\n\ntemplate <typename T>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<T>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  if (n_leading_bits_ <= 0) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n\n  uint64_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n_leading_bits_;\n\n  // Compute the harmonic mean using dense buckets and overflow buckets\n  double sum = 0.0;\n  for (uint64_t i = 0; i < num_buckets; ++i) {\n    uint64_t dense_val = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n    uint64_t overflow_val = 0;\n\n    if (overflow_bucket_.find(i) != overflow_bucket_.end()) {\n      overflow_val = overflow_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n    }\n\n    // Reconstruct the position\n    uint64_t position = dense_val | (overflow_val << 4);\n\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(position));\n  }\n\n  // Apply the HyperLogLog formula\n  double raw_estimate = CONSTANT * num_buckets * num_buckets / sum;\n\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(raw_estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<std::string>;\n}  // namespace bustub\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":25,"oldLines":19,"newStart":25,"newLines":17,"lines":["   // Compute the remaining bits (upper bits after removing bucket index bits)","   hash_t remaining_hash = hash >> (n_leading_bits_ > 0 ? n_leading_bits_ : 0);"," ","-  // Find position = leading zeros + 1 (counting from MSB)","+  // Find position = bit index + 1 (counting bit positions from the right, 0-indexed)","   uint64_t position = 0;","-  if (remaining_hash == 0) {","-    position = 65;
